**тШЕ Leviathan et al. - **bridge = step_norm/step_wall = 0.2147**; a batch=1 WALL draft saving over-credits by **4.82├Ч**. kanna #269 +4.39% тЖТ **+0.91% basis-honest**.


## Key Reference: TPS Composition

```
official = K_cal ┬╖ (E[T] / step) ┬╖ ╧Д = 125.268 ┬╖ (3.844 / 1218.2) ┬╖ 1.218 = 481.53 TPS

  K_cal = 125.268    (calibration constant)
  E[T]  = 3.844      (expected accepted tokens, K=7 linear MTP, M=8 verify)
  step  = 1218.2┬╡s   (NORMALIZED/batch-amortized composition unit тАФ NOT a wall sum, denken #278)
  ╧Д     = 1.218

To reach 500: need +3.835% (E[T] floor 3.9914). With step fully closed, the ONLY
multiplicand that can move is E[T]. Bridge-discount all batch=1 wall draft savings
by 0.2147; verify-side deployed-M=8 savings carry bridgeтЙИ1.0 (kanna #286 confirming).
```
